Automatically classifies tasks into compliance tiers and enforces appropriate verification.\n\n**Key Benefits**:\n- Single command replaces confusion between `sc:task` and `sc:task-mcp`\n- Automatic tier classification with confidence scoring\n- Appropriate verification for each task type\n- Prevents over-engineering for trivial changes\n- Ensures safety for critical changes\n\n## Triggers\n\nUse `/sc:task` when:\n- Task involves code modifications with downstream impacts\n- Complexity score >0.6 with code modifications\n- Multi-file scope (>2 estimated affected files)\n- Security domain paths detected (auth/, security/, crypto/)\n- Refactoring or system-wide changes requested\n\n**Auto-Suggest Keywords**:\n- High confidence: \"implement feature\", \"refactor system\", \"fix security\", \"add authentication\", \"update database schema\"\n- Moderate confidence: \"add new\", \"create component\", \"update service\", \"modify API\"\n\n## Usage\n\n```bash\n/sc:task [description]                           # Auto-detect all dimensions\n/sc:task [description] --compliance strict       # Force STRICT tier\n/sc:task [description] --compliance light        # Force LIGHT tier\n/sc:task [description] --skip-compliance         # Bypass compliance (escape hatch)\n/sc:task [description] --verify auto             # Auto-select verification\n```\n\n## Behavioral Flow\n\n### 0. Load context via codebase-retrieval\n2. Search downstream impacts (find_referencing_symbols OR grep)\n3. Make changes\n4. Run affected tests OR document manual verification\n5. Verify basic functionality\n\n**LIGHT Execution**:\n1. Quick scope check (files/lines within bounds)\n2. Make changes\n3. Quick sanity check (syntax valid, no obvious errors)\n4. Proceed with judgment\n\n**EXEMPT Execution**:\n1. Execute immediately\n2. No verification overhead\n\n### 4. Verification Phase\n\nRoute to appropriate verification based on tier and paths:\n\n| Compliance Tier | Verification Method | Token Cost | Timeout |\n|-----------------|---------------------|------------|---------|\n| STRICT | Sub-agent (quality-engineer) | 3-5K | 60s |\n| STANDARD | Direct test execution | 300-500 | 30s |\n| LIGHT | Skip verification | 0 | 0s |\n| EXEMPT | Skip verification | 0 | 0s |\n\n**Critical Path Override**: Paths matching `auth/`, `security/`, `crypto/`, `models/`, `migrations/` always trigger CRITICAL verification regardless of compliance tier.\n\n**Trivial Path Override**: Paths matching `*.md`, `docs/`, `*test*.py` may skip verification.\n\n### 5. TodoWrite: Create task breakdown\n2. codebase-retrieval: Load context\n3. list_memories / read_memory: Check project state\n\n**Execution Phase**:\n1. Edit/MultiEdit/Write: Make changes\n2. Grep/Glob: Find references\n3. find_referencing_symbols: Trace dependencies\n\n**Verification Phase**:\n1. Task (quality-engineer): Spawn verification agent (STRICT only)\n2. Bash: Run tests directly (STANDARD)\n3. think_about_task_adherence: Reflect on completeness\n\n**Completion Phase**:\n1. write_memory: Save session state\n2. think_about_whether_you_are_done: Final check\n\n## Examples\n\n### STRICT Task\n```\n/sc:task \"implement user authentication with JWT\"\n\n-> Classified as STRICT (security domain, authentication keyword)\n-> Full 6-category checklist classification\n-> Full verification enforced\n```\n\n## Boundaries\n\n**Will:**\n- Classify tasks into appropriate compliance tiers\n- Enforce tier-appropriate verification requirements\n- Provide Evidence-Based Development**\n    85→\n    86→**Never guess** - always verify with official sources:\n    87→- Use Context7 MCP for official documentation\n    88→- Use WebFetch/WebSearch for research\n    89→- Check existing code with Glob/Grep before implementing\n    90→- Verify assumptions against test results\n    91→\n    92→**Anti-pattern**: Implementing based on assumptions or outdated knowledge\n    93→\n    94→### **2. Confidence-First Implementation**\n    95→\n    96→Check confidence BEFORE starting work:\n    97→- **≥90%**: Proceed with implementation\n    98→- **70-89%**: Present alternatives, continue investigation\n    99→- **<70%**: STOP - ask questions, investigate more\n   100→\n   101→**ROI**: Spend 100-200 tokens on confidence check to save 5,000-50,000 tokens on wrong direction\n   102→\n   103→### **3. Parallel-First Execution**\n   104→\n   105→Use **Wave → Checkpoint → Wave** pattern:\n   106→```\n   107→Wave 1: [Read file1, Read file2, Read file3] (parallel)\n   108→   ↓\n   109→Checkpoint: Analyze all files together\n   110→   ↓\n   111→Wave 2: [Edit file1, Edit file2, Edit file3] (parallel)\n   112→```\n   113→\n   114→**Benefit**: 3.5x faster than sequential execution\n   115→\n   116→**When to use**:\n   117→- Independent operations (reading multiple files)\n   118→- Batch transformations (editing multiple files)\n   119→- Parallel searches (grep across different directories)\n   120→\n   121→**When NOT to use**:\n   122→- Operations with dependencies (must wait for previous result)\n   123→- Sequential analysis (need to build context step-by-step)\n   124→\n   125→### **4. Token Efficiency**\n   126→\n   127→Allocate tokens based on task complexity:\n   128→- **Simple** (typo fix): 200 tokens\n   129→- **Medium** (bug fix): 1,000 tokens\n   130→- **Complex** (feature): 2,500 tokens\n   131→\n   132→**Confidence check ROI**: 25-250x token savings\n   133→\n   134→### **5. No Hallucinations**\n   135→\n   136→Use SelfCheckProtocol to prevent hallucinations:\n   137→\n   138→**The Four Questions**:\n   139→1. Are all tests passing? (show output)\n   140→2. Are all requirements met? (list items)\n   141→3. No assumptions without verification? (show docs)\n   142→4. Is there evidence? (test results, code changes, validation)\n   143→\n   144→**7 Red Flags**:\n   145→- \"Tests pass\" without output\n   146→- \"Everything works\" without evidence\n   147→- \"Implementation complete\" with failing tests\n   148→- Skipping error messages\n   149→- Ignoring warnings\n   150→- Hiding failures\n   151→- \"Probably works\" language\n   152→\n   153→---\n   154→\n   155→## 🚫 **Absolute upstream document |\n    55→| 5 | Downstream Quote | String | Non-empty or `[MISSING]` | Verbatim quote from downstream document |\n    56→| 6 | Impact | String | Non-empty | Assessment of how deviation affects correctness |\n    57→| 7 | Recommended Correction | String | Non-empty | Specific action to resolve the deviation |\n    58→\n    59→## Column Name Rationale\n    60→\n len(embedded.encode(\"utf-8\")) <= _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT:\n   174→        effective_prompt = step.prompt + \"\\n\\n\" + embedded\n   175→        extra_args: list[str] = []\n   176→    elif embedded:\n   177→        _log.warning(\n   178→            \"Step '%s': embedded inputs exceed %d bytes, falling back to --file flags\",\n   179→            step.id,\n   180→            _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT,\n   181→        )\n   182→        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n   183→        extra_args = [\n   184→            arg\n   185→            for input_path in step.inputs\n   186→            for arg in    prompt=effective_prompt,\n   194→        output_file=step.output_file,\n   195→        error_file=step.output_file.with_suffix(\".err\"),\n   196→        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n   197→        model=step.model or config.model,\n   198→        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n   199→        timeout_seconds=step.timeout_seconds,\n   200→        output_format=\"text\",\n   201→        extra_args=extra_args,\n   202→    )\n   203→\n   204→    proc.start()\n   205→\n   206→    # Poll for cancellation while waiting\n   207→    while proc._process is not None and proc._process.poll() is None:\n   208→        if cancel_check():\n   209→            proc.terminate()\n   210→            return StepResult(\n   211→                step=step,\n   212→                status=StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n   213→                attempt=1,\n   214→                gate_failure_reason=\"Cancelled by external signal\",\n   215→                started_at=started_at,\n   216→                finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n   217→            )\n   218→        time.sleep(1)\n   219→\n   220→    exit_code = proc.wait()\n   221→    finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   222→\n   223→    if exit_code == 124:\n   224→        return StepResult(\n   225→            step=step,\n   226→            status=StepStatus.TIMEOUT,\n   227→ finished_at=finished_at,\n   231→        )\n   232→\n   233→    if exit_code != 0:\n   234→        return StepResult(\n   235→            step=step,\n   236→            status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n finished_at=finished_at,\n   241→        )\n   242→\n   243→    # Sanitize output: strip conversational preamble before gate validation\n   244→    _sanitize_output(step.output_file)\n   245→\n   246→ 259→\n   260→def _build_steps(config: RoadmapConfig) -> list[Step | list[Step]]:\n   261→    \"\"\"Build the 9-step pipeline with parallel generate group.\n   262→\n   263→    Returns a list where 381→\n   382→def _format_halt_output(results: list[StepResult], config: RoadmapConfig) -> str:\n   383→    \"\"\"Format HALT diagnostic output per spec section 6.2.\"\"\"\n   384→    failed = [r for r StepStatus.CANCELLED]\n   387→\n   388→    if not failed:\n   389→        return \"\"\n   390→\n   391→    fail = failed[-1]\n   392→    step = fail.step\n   393→\n   394→    # Calculate file details len(content.encode(\"utf-8\"))\n   399→        line_count = len(content.splitlines())\n   400→        file_info = f\"  Output size: {byte_count} bytes ({line_count} lines)\\n\"\n   401→    elif step:\n   402→        file_info = \"  Output file: not created\\n\"\n   403→\n   404→    elapsed = f\"{fail.duration_seconds:.0f}s\"\n   405→\n   406→    lines = [\n   407→        f\"ERROR: Roadmap pipeline halted at step '{step.id}' (attempt {fail.attempt}/2)\",\n   408→        f\"  Gate failure: {fail.gate_failure_reason}\",\n   409→        f\"  Output file: {step.output_file}\",\n   410→        file_info.rstrip(),\n   411→        f\"  Step timeout: {step.timeout_seconds}s | Elapsed: {elapsed}\",\n   412→        \"\",\n   413→        f\"Completed steps: {', '.join(f'{r.step.id} (PASS, attempt {r.attempt})' for r in passed) or 'none'}\",\n   414→        f\"Failed step:     {step.id} ({fail.status.value}, attempt {fail.attempt})\",\n   415→    ]\n   416→\n   417→    # Collect skipped steps\n   418→    all_step_ids = _get_all_step_ids(config)\n   419→    executed_ids = {r.step.id for r in results}\n   420→    skipped_ids = [sid for sid in all_step_ids if sid not in executed_ids]\n 508→\n   509→\n   510→def _save_state(config: RoadmapConfig, results: list[StepResult]) -> None:\n   511→    \"\"\"Write .roadmap-state.json to output_dir via atomic tmp + os.replace().\n   512→\n StepStatus.PASS:\n   565→        # Check if the output indicates degraded mode\n   566→        if result.step and result.step.output_file.exists():\n   567→            content = 621→\n   622→\n   623→def write_state(state: dict, path: Path) -> None:\n   624→    \"\"\"Write state dict to path atomically via tmp file + os.replace().\"\"\"\n   625→    import os as _os\n   626→\n   627→    path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n   628→    tmp = path.with_suffix(\".tmp\")\n   629→    tmp.write_text(json.dumps(state, indent=2), encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   630→  635→    if not path.exists():\n   636→        return None\n   637→    try:\n   638→        text = path.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   639→        if not text.strip():\n   640→            return list[Deliverable]) -> list[Deliverable]:\n   647→    \"\"\"Post-generation decomposition pass for the roadmap pipeline.\n   648→\n   649→    Runs after deliverable generation, before output formatting.\n   650→    Splits behavioral deliverables into Implement/Verify pairs.\n   651→\n   652→    Idempotent: running twice produces identical results because\n   653→    already-decomposed deliverables (IDs ending .a/.b) are skipped.\n   654→\n   655→    Preserves milestone-internal ordering: deliverables within each\n   656→    milestone maintain their relative order after False) -> None:\n   662→    \"\"\"Execute the roadmap generation pipeline.\n   663→\n   664→    Builds the step list, handles --dry-run and --resume, then\n   665→    delegates to execute_pipeline() with roadmap_run_step.\n   666→\n   667→    After all 9 steps pass, auto-invokes validation unless\n   668→    --no-validate is set or --resume halted on a failed step.\n   669→\n   670→    Note: --no-validate does NOT skip the spec-fidelity step\n   671→    (FR-010, AC-005). It only skips the post-pipeline validation\n   672→    subsystem.\n   673→    \"\"\"\n   674→    config.output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n   675→\n   676→    steps =  688→\n   689→    # Execute pipeline\n   690→    results = execute_pipeline(\n   691→        steps=steps,\n   692→        config=config,\n   693→        run_step=roadmap_run_step,\n   694→        on_step_start=_print_step_start,\n   695→        on_step_complete=_print_step_complete,\n   696→    )\n   697→\n   698→    # Save state\n   699→    _save_state(config, results)\n   700→\n   701→    # Check for failures\n   702→    failures = [r for r in results if r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)]\n   703→    if failures:\n   704→        halt_msg = _format_halt_output(results, config)\n   705→        print(halt_msg, file=sys.stderr)\n   706→        sys.exit(1)\n   707→\n   708→    print(f\"\\n[roadmap] Pipeline complete: {len(results)} steps passed\", flush=True)\n   709→\n   710→    # Auto-invoke validation after successful pipeline completion\n   711→    if no_validate:\n   712→        print(\"[roadmap] Validation skipped (--no-validate)\", flush=True)\n   713→        _save_validation_status(config, \"skipped\")\n   714→        return\n   715→\n   716→    # Check if validation already completed (--resume path)\n   717→    if resume:\n   718→        state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n   719→        state = read_state(state_file)\n   720→        if state and \"validation\" in state:\n   721→            saved = state[\"validation\"]\n Examples:\\n\"\n    58→        \"- A task's effort estimate diverges significantly from the roadmap\\n\"\n    59→        \"- Acceptance criteria are weaker than the roadmap's success criteria\\n\"\n    60→        \"- A dependency is acknowledged but not properly sequenced\\n\"\n    61→        \"- Verification method differs from roadmap recommendation\\n\\n\"\n    62→        \"**LOW**: Minor stylistic, formatting, or organizational differences that \"\n    63→        \"do not affect execution correctness. Uses atomic write (write to ``.tmp`` then ``os.replace()``) to prevent\n    partial file states.\n\n    Returns the byte count of the stripped preamble (0 when file already starts\n    with ``---`` or    \"\"\"\n    content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    if not content.startswith(\"---\"):\n        return\n\n    # Find end of frontmatter\n    end_idx = content.find(\"\\n---\", argv with context isolation, launches process, waits with\n    timeout, and returns StepResult.\n    \"\"\"\n    started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n    if config.dry_run:\n        _log.info(\"[dry-run] Would execute step '%s'\", step.id)\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.PASS,\n            attempt=1,\n            started_at=started_at,\n            finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n        )\n\n    # Inline embedding: read input files into the prompt instead of --file flags\n    embedded = []\n    elif embedded:\n        _log.warning(\n            \"Step '%s': embedded inputs exceed %d bytes, falling back to --file flags\",\n            step.id,\n            _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT,\n        )\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n        extra_args = [\n            arg\n            for input_path in step.inputs\n            for arg in (\"--file\", str(input_path))\n        ]\n    else:\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n        extra_args = []\n\n    proc = ClaudeProcess(\n        prompt=effective_prompt,\n        output_file=step.output_file,\n        error_file=step.output_file.with_suffix(\".err\"),\n        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n        model=step.model or config.model,\n        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n        timeout_seconds=step.timeout_seconds,\n        output_format=\"text\",\n        extra_args=extra_args,\n    )\n\n    proc.start()\n\n    # Poll for cancellation while waiting\n    while proc._process is not None and proc._process.poll() is None:\n        if cancel_check():\n            proc.terminate()\n            return StepResult(\n                step=step,\n                status=StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n                attempt=1,\n                gate_failure_reason=\"Cancelled by external signal\",\n                started_at=started_at,\n                finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n            )\n        time.sleep(1)\n\n    exit_code = proc.wait()\n    finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n    if exit_code == 124:\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.TIMEOUT,\n            attempt=1,\n            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' timed out after {step.timeout_seconds}s\",\n            started_at=started_at,\n            finished_at=finished_at,\n        )\n\n    if exit_code != 0:\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n This document specifies the conservative merge protocol\nfor future implementation.\n\n## Conservative Merge Protocol\n\n### Rule 1: Highest Severity Wins\n\nWhen multiple agents report severity assessments for the same deviation:\n\n| Agent A | Agent B | Resolved Severity |\n|---------|---------|-------------------|\n| HIGH    | MEDIUM  | HIGH              |\n| MEDIUM  | LOW     | MEDIUM            |\n| HIGH    | LOW     | HIGH              |\n| HIGH    | HIGH    | HIGH              |\n\n**Rationale**: Conservative merge ensures no genuine issue is downgraded. False\npositives are preferred over false negatives for safety-critical pipeline gates.\n\n### Rule 2: validation_complete Semantics\n\n| Condition | validation_complete |\n|-----------|---------------------|\n| All agents succeed | `true` |\n| Any agent fails | `false` |\n| Any agent times out | `false` |\n| Any agent produces invalid output | `false` |\n\nWhen `validation_complete: false`, the pipeline emits a **degraded** status\n(not a hard failure), preserving successful agent results while clearly\nflagging incomplete validation.\n\n### Rule 3: Failure Handling\n\n1. **Agent timeout**: Record timeout as failure; emit warning with agent ID\n2. **Invalid output**: Record as failure; preserve raw output for debugging\n3. **Partial results**: Merge available results; flag missing agents in report\n4. **All agents fail**: Set `validation_complete: false`; `tasklist_ready: false`\n\n### Rule 4: Merge Order\n\n1. Collect per-agent deviation tables\n2. Deduplicate by deviation ID (same upstream/downstream quote pair)\n3. For duplicates: apply Rule 1 (highest severity wins)\n4. For unique deviations: include as-is\n5. Compute aggregate counts from merged table\n\n## Deferral Notice\n\nFull implementation of FR-012 multi-agent severity resolution is deferred to\n**v2.21 (RoadmapRemediate)**. Unresolved references emit warnings but\n    42→    do not block the pipeline (warning-only mode per OQ-001 for v2.20).\n    43→    \"\"\"\n    44→    import re\n    45→    import warnings\n    46→\n    47→    # Check each reference against headings\n    62→    unresolved: list[str] = []\n    63→    for ref in refs:\n    64→        found = any(ref in h for h in headings)\n    65→        if not found:\n    66→            # Also check if the section number appears as a heading prefix\n    67→            found = any(h.startswith(ref) for h in headings)\n    68→        if not found:\n    69→            unresolved.append(ref)\n    70→\n    71→    if unresolved:\n    72→        for ref in unresolved:\n    73→            warnings.warn(\n    74→                f\"Unresolved cross-reference: 'See section {ref}' has no matching heading\",\n    75→                stacklevel=2,\n    76→            )\n    77→        # Returns False if:\n   157→    - Frontmatter is missing\n   158→    - high_severity_count field is missing\n   159→    - high_severity_count > 0\n   160→\n   161→    Raises TypeError if high_severity_count value is not parseable as an integer.\n   162→    \"\"\"\n   163→    fm = _parse_frontmatter(content)\n   164→    if fm is None:\n   165→        return False\n   166→\n   167→    value = fm.get(\"high_severity_count\")\n   168→    if value is None:\n   169→        return False\n   170→\n   171→    try:\n   172→        count = int(value)\n   173→    except (ValueError, TypeError):\n   174→        raise TypeError(\n   175→            f\"high_severity_count must be an integer, got: {value!r}\"\n   176→        )\n   177→\n   178→    return count == 0\n   179→\n   180→\n   181→def _tasklist_ready_consistent(content: str) -> bool:\n   182→    \"\"\"Validate tasklist_ready is consistent with severity counts.\n   183→\n   184→    Consistency rule: tasklist_ready=true requires high_severity_count=0\n   185→    AND validation_complete=true. Full body of the actual gate validator\n\nFile:\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/gates.py`\n\nFunction signature:\n```python\ndef gate_passed(output_file: Path, criteria: GateCriteria) -> tuple[bool, str | None]:\n```\n\nFull body:\n```python\ndef gate_passed(output_file: Path, criteria: GateCriteria) -> tuple[bool, str | None]:\n    \"\"\"Validate a step's output against its gate criteria.\n\n    Returns (True, None) on pass.\n    Returns (False, reason) on failure where reason is human-readable.\n    \"\"\"\n    tier = criteria.enforcement_tier\n\n    # EXEMPT: always passes\n    if tier == \"EXEMPT\":\n        return True, None\n\n    # LIGHT, STANDARD, STRICT: file must exist\n    if not output_file.exists():\n        return False, f\"File not found: {output_file}\"\n\n    # LIGHT, STANDARD, STRICT: file must be non-empty\n    content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    if len(content.strip()) == 0:\n        return False, f\"File empty (0 bytes): {output_file}\"\n\n    # LIGHT stops here\n    if tier == \"LIGHT\":\n        return True, None\n\n    # STANDARD, STRICT: minimum line count\n    lines = content.splitlines()\n    if len(lines) < criteria.min_lines:\n        return False, (\n            f\"Below minimum line count: {len(lines)} < {criteria.min_lines} \"\n            f\"in {output_file}\"\n        )\n\n    # STANDARD, STRICT: YAML frontmatter fields\n    if criteria.required_frontmatter_fields:\n        ok, reason = _check_frontmatter(content, criteria.required_frontmatter_fields, output_file)\n        if not ok:\n            return False, reason\n\n    # STANDARD stops here\n    if tier == \"STANDARD\":\n        return True, None\n\n    # STRICT: semantic checks\n    if criteria.semantic_checks:\n        for check in criteria.semantic_checks:\n            if not check.check_fn(content):\n                return False, f\"Semantic check '{check.name}' failed: {check.failure_message}\"\n\n    return True, None\n```\n\nSupporting frontmatter checker:\n```python\ndef _check_frontmatter(\n    content: str, required_fields: list[str], output_file: Path\n) -> tuple[bool, str | None]:\n    \"\"\"Extract and validate YAML frontmatter fields.\n\n    Uses regex with re.MULTILINE to discover frontmatter anywhere in the\n    document (not just byte 0), allowing conversational preamble before the\n    ``---`` delimiters.  Horizontal rules (``---`` with no ``key: value``\n    content) are rejected because the pattern requires at least one\n    ``key: value`` line between delimiters.\n    \"\"\"\n    match = _FRONTMATTER_RE.search(content)\n    if match is None:\n        return False, f\"YAML frontmatter not found in {output_file}\"\n\n    frontmatter_text = match.group(1)\n\n    # Extract keys from key: value lines\n    found_keys: set[str] = set()\n    for line in frontmatter_text.splitlines():\n        line = line.strip()\n        if \":\" in line:\n            key = line.split(\":\", 1)[0].strip()\n            if key:\n                found_keys.add(key)\n\n    for field in required_fields:\n        if field not in found_keys:\n            return False, f\"Missing required frontmatter field '{field}' in {output_file}\"\n\n    return True, None\n```\n\nImportant implementation detail:\n- `_FRONTMATTER_RE` uses `.search()`, not `.match()`, so frontmatter can appear after conversational preamble or blank lines.\n\n## 3. `GateCriteria` dataclass\n\nFile:\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/models.py`\n\nDefinition:\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass GateCriteria:\n    \"\"\"Defines what constitutes a passing output for a pipeline step.\"\"\"\n\n    required_frontmatter_fields: list[str]\n    min_lines: int\n    enforcement_tier: Literal[\"STRICT\", \"STANDARD\", \"LIGHT\", \"EXEMPT\"] = \"STANDARD\"\n    semantic_checks: list[SemanticCheck] | None = None\n```\n\nRelated type:\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass SemanticCheck:\n    \"\"\"Pure Python check applied to file content. Full body of the actual gate validator\n\nFile:\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/gates.py`\n\nFunction signature:\n```python\ndef gate_passed(output_file: Path, criteria: GateCriteria) -> tuple[bool, str | None]:\n```\n\nFull body:\n```python\ndef gate_passed(output_file: Path, criteria: GateCriteria) -> tuple[bool, str | None]:\n    \"\"\"Validate a step's output against its gate criteria.\n\n    Returns (True, None) on pass.\n    Returns (False, reason) on failure where reason is human-readable.\n    \"\"\"\n    tier = criteria.enforcement_tier\n\n    # EXEMPT: always passes\n    if tier == \"EXEMPT\":\n        return True, None\n\n    # LIGHT, STANDARD, STRICT: file must exist\n    if not output_file.exists():\n        return False, f\"File not found: {output_file}\"\n\n    # LIGHT, STANDARD, STRICT: file must be non-empty\n    content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    if len(content.strip()) == 0:\n        return False, f\"File empty (0 bytes): {output_file}\"\n\n    # LIGHT stops here\n    if tier == \"LIGHT\":\n        return True, None\n\n    # STANDARD, STRICT: minimum line count\n    lines = content.splitlines()\n    if len(lines) < criteria.min_lines:\n        return False, (\n            f\"Below minimum line count: {len(lines)} < {criteria.min_lines} \"\n            f\"in {output_file}\"\n        )\n\n    # STANDARD, STRICT: YAML frontmatter fields\n    if criteria.required_frontmatter_fields:\n        ok, reason = _check_frontmatter(content, criteria.required_frontmatter_fields, output_file)\n        if not ok:\n            return False, reason\n\n    # STANDARD stops here\n    if tier == \"STANDARD\":\n        return True, None\n\n    # STRICT: semantic checks\n    if criteria.semantic_checks:\n        for check in criteria.semantic_checks:\n            if not check.check_fn(content):\n                return False, f\"Semantic check '{check.name}' failed: {check.failure_message}\"\n\n    return True, None\n```\n\nSupporting frontmatter checker:\n```python\ndef _check_frontmatter(\n    content: str, required_fields: list[str], output_file: Path\n) -> tuple[bool, str | None]:\n    \"\"\"Extract and validate YAML frontmatter fields.\n\n    Uses regex with re.MULTILINE to discover frontmatter anywhere in the\n    document (not just byte 0), allowing conversational preamble before the\n    ``---`` delimiters.  Horizontal rules (``---`` with no ``key: value``\n    content) are rejected because the pattern requires at least one\n    ``key: value`` line between delimiters.\n    \"\"\"\n    match = _FRONTMATTER_RE.search(content)\n    if match is None:\n        return False, f\"YAML frontmatter not found in {output_file}\"\n\n    frontmatter_text = match.group(1)\n\n    # Extract keys from key: value lines\n    found_keys: set[str] = set()\n    for line in frontmatter_text.splitlines():\n        line = line.strip()\n        if \":\" in line:\n            key = line.split(\":\", 1)[0].strip()\n            if key:\n                found_keys.add(key)\n\n    for field in required_fields:\n        if field not in found_keys:\n            return False, f\"Missing required frontmatter field '{field}' in {output_file}\"\n\n    return True, None\n```\n\nImportant implementation detail:\n- `_FRONTMATTER_RE` uses `.search()`, not `.match()`, so frontmatter can appear after conversational preamble or blank lines.\n\n## 3. `GateCriteria` dataclass\n\nFile:\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/models.py`\n\nDefinition:\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass GateCriteria:\n    \"\"\"Defines what constitutes a passing output for a pipeline step.\"\"\"\n\n    required_frontmatter_fields: list[str]\n    min_lines: int\n    enforcement_tier: Literal[\"STRICT\", \"STANDARD\", \"LIGHT\", \"EXEMPT\"] = \"STANDARD\"\n    semantic_checks: list[SemanticCheck] | None = None\n```\n\nRelated type:\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass SemanticCheck:\n    \"\"\"Pure Python check applied to file content. No LLM invocation.\"\"\"\n\n    name: str\n    check_fn: Callable[[str], bool]\n    failure_message: str\n```\n\n## 4. These statuses are mutually exclusive and visually\ndistinguishable in pipeline output.\n\n## Status Definitions\n\n### PASS\n\n| Property | Value |\n|----------|-------|\n| **Definition** | Step completed successfully and output passed all gate criteria |\n| **Trigger Conditions** | Gate returns `(True, None)` for all checks |\n| **Pipeline Output** | `[step-id] PASS` (green in terminal) |\n| **User Action** | None required — proceed to next step |\n| **Example** | `[extract] PASS — 13 frontmatter fields present, 127 lines` |\n\n### FAIL\n\n| Property | Value |\n|----------|-------|\n| **Definition** | Step completed but output did not pass gate criteria after all retries |\n| **Trigger Conditions** | Gate returns `(False, reason)` and retry_limit exhausted |\n| **Pipeline Output** | `[step-id] FAIL: <reason>` (red in terminal) |\n| **User Action** | Investigate failure reason; fix upstream input; re-run with `--resume` |\n| **Example** | `[merge] FAIL: Missing required frontmatter field 'adversarial'` |\n\n### SKIPPED\n\n| Property | Value |\n|----------|-------|\n| **Definition** | Step was not executed because its output already passes the gate |\n| **Trigger Conditions** | `--resume` mode and existing output passes gate; OR `--no-validate` for post-pipeline validation |\n| **Pipeline Output** | `[step-id] SKIP (output already passes gate)` |\n| **User Action** | None required — previous output is still valid |\n| **Example** | `[extract] SKIP (output already passes gate)` |\n\n### DEGRADED\n\n| Property | Value |\n|----------|-------|\n| **Definition** | Step produced partial results; some sub-components succeeded but not all |\n| **Trigger Conditions** | Multi-agent validation where at least one agent succeeds but another fails or times out |\n| **Pipeline Output** | `[validate] DEGRADED: agents failed: [haiku-qa]` |\n| **User Action** | Review successful agent results; decide whether to accept partial validation or re-run failed agents |\n| **Example** | `[validate] DEGRADED — opus-architect succeeded, haiku-qa timed out` |\n\n## State Distinguishability\n\n| Status | Color | Icon | Frontmatter Field |\n|--------|-------|------|-------------------|\n| PASS | Green | (none) | `validation_complete: true` |\n| FAIL | Red | (none) | `validation_complete: false`, `tasklist_ready: false` |\n| SKIPPED | Yellow | (none) | `validation_complete: skipped` |\n| DEGRADED | Yellow | (none) | `validation_complete: false` (partial results preserved) |\n\n## Implementation References\n\n- Step status enum: `src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/models.py` (`StepStatus`)\n- Gate checking: `src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/gates.py` (`gate_passed()`)\n- Degraded report: `src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/validate_executor.py` (`_write_degraded_report()`)\n- Skip logic: `src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/executor.py` (resume handling)\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":5321,"cache_read_input_tokens":126779,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":5321,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"83953bef-fc9e-4290-9031-c4f2babaa3bb","uuid":"37f7f6d5-e82c-4911-beb7-7d078d323753"}

Auto-loaded by pytest\n│   ├── pm_agent/                  # Pre/post implementation patterns\n│   │   ├── confidence.py          # Pre-execution confidence check\n│   │   ├── self_check.py          # Post-implementation validation\n│   │   ├── reflexion.py           # Error learning\n│   │   └── token_budget.py        # Token allocation\n│   ├── execution/                 # Parallel execution\n│   │   ├── parallel.py            # Wave→Checkpoint→Wave\n│   │   ├── reflection.py          # Meta-reasoning\n│   │   └── self_correction.py     # Error recovery\n│   └── cli/                       # Command-line interface\n│       ├── main.py                # superclaude command\n│       ├── doctor.py              # Health checks\n│       └── install_skill.py       # Skill installation\n│\n├── Plugin Source (plugins/superclaude/)  # v5.0 - NOT ACTIVE YET\n│   ├── agents/                    # Agent definitions\n│   ├── commands/                  # Command definitions\n│   ├── hooks/                     # Hook configurations\n│   ├── scripts/                   # Shell scripts\n│   └── skills/                    # Skill implementations\n│\n├── Tests (tests/)\n│   ├── unit/                      # Component unit tests\n│   └── integration/               # Plugin integration tests\n│\n└── Documentation (docs/)\n    ├── architecture/              # Architecture decisions\n    ├── developer-guide/           # Development guides\n    ├── reference/                 # API reference\n    ├── research/                  # Research findings\n    └── user-guide/                # User documentation\n```\n\n### **Future State (v5.0 - Planned)**\n\n- TypeScript plugin system (issue #419)\n- Project-local `.claude-plugin/` detection\n- Plugin marketplace distribution\n- Enhanced MCP server integration\n\n---\n\n## ⚙️ **Design Principles**\n\n### **1. Evidence-Based Development**\n\n**Never guess** - always verify with official sources:\n- Use Context7 MCP for official documentation\n- Use WebFetch/WebSearch for research\n- Check existing code with Glob/Grep before implementing\n- Verify assumptions against test results\n\n**Anti-pattern**: Implementing based on assumptions or outdated knowledge\n\n### **2. Confidence-First Implementation**\n\nCheck confidence BEFORE starting work:\n- **≥90%**: Proceed with implementation\n- **70-89%**: Present alternatives, continue investigation\n- **<70%**: STOP - ask questions, investigate more\n\n**ROI**: Spend 100-200 tokens on confidence check to save 5,000-50,000 tokens on wrong direction\n\n### **3. Parallel-First Execution**\n\nUse **Wave → Checkpoint → Wave** pattern:\n```\nWave 1: [Read file1, Read file2, Read file3] (parallel)\n   ↓\nCheckpoint: Analyze all files together\n   ↓\nWave 2: [Edit file1, Edit file2, Edit file3] (parallel)\n```\n\n**Benefit**: 3.5x faster than sequential execution\n\n**When to use**:\n- Independent operations (reading multiple files)\n- Batch transformations (editing multiple files)\n- Parallel searches (grep across different directories)\n\n**When NOT to use**:\n- Operations with dependencies (must wait for previous result)\n- Sequential analysis (need to build context step-by-step)\n\n### **4. Token Efficiency**\n\nAllocate tokens based on task complexity:\n- **Simple** (typo fix): 200 tokens\n- **Medium** (bug fix): 1,000 tokens\n- **Complex** (feature): 2,500 tokens\n\n**Confidence check ROI**: 25-250x token savings\n\n### **5. No Hallucinations**\n\nUse SelfCheckProtocol to prevent hallucinations:\n\n**The Four Questions**:\n1. Are all tests passing? (show output)\n2. Are all requirements met? (list items)\n3. No assumptions without verification? (show docs)\n4. Is there evidence? (test results, code changes, validation)\n\n**7 Red Flags**:\n- \"Tests pass\" without output\n- \"Everything works\" without evidence\n- \"Implementation complete\" with failing tests\n- Skipping error messages\n- Ignoring warnings\n- Hiding failures\n- \"Probably works\" language\n\n---\n\n## 🚫 **Absolute Rules**\n\n### **Python Environment**\n\n1. **ALWAYS use UV** for Python operations:\n   ```bash\n   uv run pytest              # NOT: python -m pytest\n   uv pip install package     # NOT: pip install package\n   uv run python script.py    # NOT: python script.py\n   ```\n\n2. **Package structure**: Use src/ layout\n   - `src/superclaude/` for package code\n   - `tests/` for test code\n   - Never mix source and tests in same directory\n\n3. **Entry points**: Use pyproject.toml\n   - CLI: `[project.scripts]`\n   - Pytest plugin: `[project.entry-points.pytest11]`\n\n### **Testing**\n\n1. **All new features MUST have tests**\n   - Unit tests for individual components\n   - Integration tests for component interactions\n   - Use pytest markers: `@pytest.mark.unit`, `@pytest.mark.integration`\n\n2. **Use PM Agent patterns in tests**:\n   ```python\n   @pytest.mark.confidence_check\n   def test_feature(confidence_checker):\n       context = {...}\n       assert confidence_checker.assess(context) >= 0.7\n\n   @pytest.mark.self_check\n   def test_implementation(self_check_protocol):\n       passed, issues = self_check_protocol.validate(impl)\n       assert passed\n   ```\n\n3. **Test fixtures**: Use conftest.py for shared fixtures\n\n### **Git Workflow**\n\n1. **Branch structure**:\n   - `master`: Production-ready code\n   - `integration`: Testing ground (not yet created)\n   - `feature/*`, `fix/*`, `docs/*`: Feature branches\n\n2. **Commit messages**: Use conventional commits\n   - `feat:` - New feature\n   - `fix:` - Bug fix\n   - `docs:` - Documentation\n   - `refactor:` - Code refactoring\n   - `test:` - Adding tests\n   - `chore:` - Maintenance\n\n3. **Never commit**:\n   - `__pycache__/`, `*.pyc`\n   - `.venv/`, `venv/`\n   - Personal files (TODO.txt, CRUSH.md)\n   - API keys, secrets\n\n### **Documentation**\n\n1. **Code documentation**:\n   - All public functions need docstrings\n   - Use type hints\n   - Include usage examples in docstrings\n\n2. **Project documentation**:\n   - Update CLAUDE.md for Claude Code guidance\n   - Update README.md for user instructions\n   - Update this PLANNING.md for architecture decisions\n   - Update TASK.md for current work\n   - Update KNOWLEDGE.md for insights\n\n3. **Keep docs synchronized**:\n   - When code changes, update relevant docs\n   - When features are added, update CHANGELOG.md\n   - When architecture changes, update PLANNING.md\n\n### **Version Management**\n\n1. **Version sources of truth**:\n   - Framework version: `VERSION` file (e.g., 4.2.0)\n   - Python package version: `pyproject.toml` (e.g., 0.4.0)\n   - NPM package version: `package.json` (should match VERSION)\n\n2. **When to bump versions**:\n   - Major: Breaking API changes\n   - Minor: New features, backward compatible\n   - Patch: Bug fixes\n\n---\n\n## 🔄 **Development Workflow**\n\n### **Starting a New Feature**\n\n1. **Investigation Phase**:\n   - Read PLANNING.md, TASK.md, KNOWLEDGE.md\n   - Check for duplicates (Glob/Grep existing code)\n   - Read official docs (Context7 MCP, WebFetch)\n   - Search for OSS implementations (WebSearch)\n   - Run confidence check (should be ≥90%)\n\n2. **Implementation Phase**:\n   - Create feature branch: `git checkout -b feature/feature-name`\n   - Write tests first (TDD)\n   - Implement feature\n   - Run tests: `uv run pytest`\n   - Run linter: `make lint`\n   - Format code: `make format`\n\n3. **Validation Phase**:\n   - Run self-check protocol\n   - Verify all tests passing\n   - Check all requirements met\n   - Confirm assumptions verified\n   - Provide evidence\n\n4. **Documentation Phase**:\n   - Update relevant documentation\n   - Add docstrings\n   - Update CHANGELOG.md\n   - Update TASK.md (mark complete)\n\n5. **Review Phase**:\n   - Create pull request\n   - Request review\n   - Address feedback\n   - Merge to integration (or master if no integration branch)\n\n### **Fixing a Bug**\n\n1. **Root Cause Analysis**:\n   - Reproduce the bug\n   - Identify root cause (not symptoms)\n   - Check reflexion memory for similar patterns\n   - Run confidence check\n\n2. **Fix Implementation**:\n   - Write failing test that reproduces bug\n   - Implement fix\n   - Verify test passes\n   - Run full test suite\n   - Record in reflexion memory\n\n3. **Prevention**:\n   - Add regression test\n   - Update documentation if needed\n   - Share learnings in KNOWLEDGE.md\n\n---\n\n## 📊 **Quality Metrics**\n\n### **Code Quality**\n\n- **Test coverage**: Aim for >80%\n- **Linting**: Zero ruff errors\n- **Type checking**: Use type hints, minimal mypy errors\n- **Documentation**: All public APIs documented\n\n### **PM Agent Metrics**\n\n- **Confidence check ROI**: 25-250x token savings\n- **Self-check detection**: 94% hallucination detection rate\n- **Parallel execution**: 3.5x speedup vs sequential\n- **Token efficiency**: 30-50% reduction with proper budgeting\n\n### **Release Criteria**\n\nBefore releasing a new version:\n- ✅ All tests passing\n- ✅ Documentation updated\n- ✅ CHANGELOG.md updated\n- ✅ Version numbers synced\n- ✅ No known critical bugs\n- ✅ Security audit passed (if applicable)\n\n---\n\n## 🚀 **Roadmap**\n\n### | Column | Type | Constraints | Description |\n|---|---|---|---|---|\n| 1 | ID | String | Format: `DEV-NNN` | Unique deviation identifier, zero-padded 3-digit |\n| 2 | Severity | Enum | `HIGH` \\| `MEDIUM` \\| `LOW` | Classification level |\n| 3 | Deviation | String | Non-empty | Concise description of what differs |\n| 4 | Upstream Quote | String | Non-empty | Verbatim quote from upstream document |\n| 5 | Downstream Quote | String | Non-empty or `[MISSING]` | Verbatim quote from downstream document |\n| 6 | Impact | String | Non-empty | Assessment of how deviation affects correctness |\n| 7 | Recommended Correction | String | Non-empty | Specific action to resolve the deviation |\n\n## Column Name Rationale\n\nGeneric names `Upstream Quote` / `Downstream Quote` are used instead of `Spec Quote` / `Roadmap Quote` because the fidelity check is reusable across document pairs (spec→roadmap, roadmap→tasklist). All consumers MUST conform to this schema.\n\n| Field | Value |\n|---|---|\n| Schema Version | 1.0 |\n| Source Decision | D-0003 (OQ-006) |\n| Effective Release | v2.20 WorkflowEvolution |\n\n## YAML Frontmatter\n\nEvery deviation report begins with YAML frontmatter:\n\n```yaml\n---\nsource_pair: \"<upstream_file> → <downstream_file>\"\nupstream_file: \"<path to upstream document>\"\ndownstream_file: \"<path to downstream document>\"\nhigh_severity_count: <integer>\nmedium_severity_count: <integer>\nlow_severity_count: <integer>\ntotal_deviations: <integer>\nvalidation_complete: <boolean>\nfidelity_check_attempted: <boolean>\ntasklist_ready: <boolean>\n---\n```\n\n### Frontmatter Field Definitions\n\n| Field | Type | Required | Description |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `source_pair` | String | Yes | Human-readable label: `\"<upstream> → <downstream>\"` |\n| `upstream_file` | String | Yes | Relative path to the upstream (source/spec) document |\n| `downstream_file` | String | Yes | Relative path to the downstream (generated) document |\n| `high_severity_count` | Integer | Yes | Count of HIGH-severity deviations (≥0) |\n| `medium_severity_count` | Integer | Yes | Count of MEDIUM-severity deviations (≥0) |\n| `low_severity_count` | Integer | Yes | Count of LOW-severity deviations (≥0) |\n| `total_deviations` | Integer | Yes | Total deviation count (must equal sum of severity counts) |\n| `validation_complete` | Boolean | Yes | `true` if the fidelity check completed without errors |\n| `fidelity_check_attempted` | Boolean | Yes | `true` if the fidelity check was invoked |\n| `tasklist_ready` | Boolean | Yes | `true` only if `high_severity_count == 0` AND `validation_complete == true` |\n\n## Deviation Table Schema (7 Columns)\n\nThe deviation table uses standard Markdown table format:\n\n| # | Column | Type | Constraints | Description |\n|---|---|---|---|---|\n| 1 | ID | String | Format: `DEV-NNN` | Unique deviation identifier, zero-padded 3-digit |\n| 2 | Severity | Enum | `HIGH` \\| `MEDIUM` \\| `LOW` | Classification level |\n| 3 | Deviation | String | Non-empty | Concise description of what differs |\n| 4 | Upstream Quote | String | Non-empty | Verbatim quote from upstream document |\n| 5 | Downstream Quote | String | Non-empty or `[MISSING]` | Verbatim quote from downstream document |\n| 6 | Impact | String | Non-empty | Assessment of how deviation affects correctness |\n| 7 | Recommended Correction | String | Non-empty | Specific action to resolve the deviation |\n\n## Column Name Rationale\n\nGeneric names `Upstream Quote` / `Downstream Quote` are used instead of `Spec Quote` / `Roadmap Quote` because the fidelity check is reusable across document pairs (spec→roadmap, roadmap→tasklist). The frontmatter `source_pair` field provides specific document context.\n\n## Gate Interactions\n\n| Gate Check | Field Used | Logic | Blocking in v2.20 |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `_high_severity_count_zero()` | `high_severity_count` | `True` if value is `0`; `False` if missing or >0 | Yes |\n| `_tasklist_ready_consistent()` | `tasklist_ready`, `high_severity_count`, `validation_complete` | `True` if consistent | Yes |\n| Count cross-validation | All severity counts vs table rows | Warning log on mismatch | No (warning only) |\n\n## Example\n\n```markdown\n---\nsource_pair: \"spec.md → roadmap.md\"\nupstream_file: \"spec.md\"\ndownstream_file: \"roadmap.md\"\nhigh_severity_count: 1\nmedium_severity_count: 2\nlow_severity_count: 0\ntotal_deviations: 3\nvalidation_complete: true\nfidelity_check_attempted: true\ntasklist_ready: false\n---\n\n# Deviation Report: spec.md → roadmap.md\n\n| ID | Severity | Deviation | Upstream Quote | Downstream Quote | Impact | Recommended Correction |\n|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|\n| DEV-001 | HIGH | Missing FR-019 | \"Cross-references must be validated\" | [MISSING] | No cross-ref integrity | Add FR-019 to Phase 2 |\n| DEV-002 | MEDIUM | NFR timeout relaxed | \"120s hard limit\" | \"120s target, 600s timeout\" | Less strict measurement | Clarify per OQ-008 |\n| DEV-003 | MEDIUM | Parameter renamed | \"spec_file\" | \"source_file\" | Import paths affected | Rename for consistency |\n```\n\n## Versioning\n\nSchema version 1.0, effective for v2.20. No HIGH-severity deviations found.\nZero unexpected issues.\n\n**Output indicators**:\n- `tasklist_ready: true` in frontmatter\n- `high_severity_count: 0`\n- `validation_complete: true`\n\n**User action**: Proceed to next phase or mark release as validated.\n\n### FAIL — Validation Failed\n\n**What it means**: Gate criteria not met after all retries. At least one check\nfailed (missing frontmatter, line count too low, or semantic check failure).\n\n**Output indicators**:\n- Error message in pipeline output: `[step-id] FAIL: <reason>`\n- `tasklist_ready: false` (if fidelity step)\n- Non-zero `high_severity_count`\n\n**User action**: Read the failure reason, fix the upstream document, and re-run\nwith `--resume` to skip already-passed steps.\n\n### SKIPPED — Already Validated\n\n**What it means**: Step was not executed because its output already exists and\npasses the gate (during `--resume`). Or post-pipeline validation was skipped\ndue to `--no-validate`.\n\n**Output indicators**:\n- `[step-id] SKIP (output already passes gate)`\n- `validation_complete: skipped` (for post-pipeline validate)\n\n**User action**: None required. Previous output is still valid.\n\n### DEGRADED — Partial Results\n\n**What it means**: Multi-agent validation where at least one agent succeeded\nbut another failed or timed out. Results from successful agents are preserved.\n\n**Output indicators**:\n- `[validate] DEGRADED: agents failed: [agent-ids]`\n- `validation_complete: false`\n- Successful agent reports still present in output directory\n\n**User action**: Review successful agent results.
